ERR-ANALYS The main systematic uncertainties sum up 9% and arise  T011000100020 
           from:                                                  T011000100021 
           . neutron detector efficiency (7%),                    T011000100022 
           . effective target thickness due to inhomogeneities andT011000100023 
             uncertainties of the energy-range tables (5%),       T011000100024 
           . incomplete beam current integration (3%),            T011000100025 
           To this number the uncertainty in background           T011000100026 
            subtraction less or equal 5%, but higher at 3.5 degreeT011000100027 
            and statistical uncertainties that depend on target,  T011000100028 
            angle, neutron energy have to be added.               T011000100029 
           (EN-ERR) Uncertainty in energy.                        T011000100030 
            Neutron energy errors for neutron actually stemming   T011000100031 
            from second chance emission are at most equal to the  T011000100032 
            recoil correction for the highest possible nucleon    T011000100033 
            energy allowing for secondary emission of neutrons    T011000100034 
            with energies above the detector threshold.           T011000100035
